      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 3rd century BC
       </b>
       . During the period 300 to 201 BC there were 226
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 83 were partial, 62 were annular (one
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 57 were total (two non-central), and 24 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, in 298 BC, 233 BC, and 211 BC.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div style="clear:both;">
      </div>
